# Text Elements
ARABIA ^ns60V4lz

Jacobite  Christians ^ZhGcl36u

- The Christians of Arabia
- Used to visit the Prophet
- Drew pictures of the youth, sometimes with a dog sleeping
with them ^rJVzcMUV

The 7 Sleepers (Youth) ^q1bRpmk7

- They were imprisoned due to not bowing 
to idols when commanded to
- They escaped and took refuge in a cave
- In Christianity, they are believed to be
martyrs ^i6XLyUhM
